The classes Receive and Send encapsulate the incoming and outgoing transmission of bytes. A Handler\\n22: is a mapping between a Receive and a Send, and represents the users hook to add logic for mapping requests\\n23: to actual processing code. Any uncaught exceptions in the reading or writing of the transmissions will result in \\n24: the server logging an error and closing the offending socket. As a result it is the duty of the Handler\\n25: implementation to catch and serialize any application-level errors that should be sent to the client.\\n26:
